## TOPIC 02256: DAQmx_ChangeDetect_DI_Tristate

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__timing__change__detection__digital__input_1gafd331264cde9d0c47fcdabafb845d20d.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__timing__change__detection__digital__input_1gafd331264cde9d0c47fcdabafb845d20d.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_ChangeDetect_DI_TristateRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies whether to tristate lines specified with Rising Edge Physical Channels and Falling Edge Physical Channels that are not in a virtual channel in the task. If you set this property to TRUE, NI-DAQmx tristates ris

### DAQmx_ChangeDetect_DI_Tristate

#### Syntax

DAQmx_ChangeDetect_DI_Tristate

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies whether to tristate lines specified with Rising Edge Physical Channels and Falling Edge Physical Channels that are not in a virtual channel in the task. If you set this property to TRUE, NI-DAQmx tristates rising/falling edge lines that are not in a virtual channel in the task. If you set this property to FALSE, NI-DAQmx does not modify the configuration of rising/falling edge lines that are not in a virtual channel in the task, even if the lines were previously tristated. Set this property to FALSE to detect changes on lines in other tasks or to detect changes on output-only lines. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetChangeDetectDITristate](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga215e54641280e6aae5d2014af81ae596.html)
- [DAQmxSetChangeDetectDITristate](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga5ea304593c9cc66dded1e993b073c053.html)
- [DAQmxResetChangeDetectDITristate](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga0673c55b49172010987c5c5416e4aca5.html)

Parent topic:

Digital Input

## TOPIC 02258: DAQmx_Hshk_StartCond

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__timing__handshake_1ga786813426037569921337256fb6f219b.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__timing__handshake_1ga786813426037569921337256fb6f219b.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_Hshk_StartCondRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the point in the handshake cycle that the device is in when the task starts.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_Immediate10198Device is waiting for space in the FIFO (for acquisition) or waiting for samples (for generation).DAQmx_Val_

### DAQmx_Hshk_StartCond

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Hshk_StartCond

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the point in the handshake cycle that the device is in when the task starts. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_Immediate | 10198 | Device is waiting for space in the FIFO (for acquisition) or waiting for samples (for generation). |
| DAQmx_Val_WaitForHandshakeTriggerAssert | 12550 | Device is waiting for the Handshake Trigger to assert. |
| DAQmx_Val_WaitForHandshakeTriggerDeassert | 12551 | Device is waiting for the Handshake Trigger to deassert. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetHshkStartCond](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga40a000f7e8f26b379c59dfc595a01af5.html)
- [DAQmxSetHshkStartCond](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga28c23216f1ca1794a2ee860dc212a1ff.html)
- [DAQmxResetHshkStartCond](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gae45cdbae35293344ad5cacd982073095.html)

Parent topic:

DAQmx_Hshk_SampleInputDataWhen

## TOPIC 02261: DAQmx_Implicit_UnderflowBehavior

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__timing__implicit_1ga5e21415f50f870a3d2d9fc3f712ff0d1.html`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_Implicit_UnderflowBehaviorRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the action to take when the onboard memory of the device becomes empty.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_HaltOutputAndError14615Stop generating samples and return an error.DAQmx_Val_PauseUntilDataAvailable14616Pause the

### DAQmx_Implicit_UnderflowBehavior

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Implicit_UnderflowBehavior

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the action to take when the onboard memory of the device becomes empty. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_HaltOutputAndError | 14615 | Stop generating samples and return an error. |
| DAQmx_Val_PauseUntilDataAvailable | 14616 | Pause the task until samples are available in the FIFO. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetImplicitUnderflowBehavior](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gab00aba49539a7b4c6a662d5f5e4a1df7.html)
- [DAQmxSetImplicitUnderflowBehavior](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga4115beeff4fd8e5255e4c2cbfab232ce.html)
- [DAQmxResetImplicitUnderflowBehavior](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga09484d4be707a32ee2012160290b6f70.html)

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AIConv_Timebase_SrcRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the terminal of the signal to use as the AI Convert Clock Timebase.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_SameAsSampTimebase10284Use the same source as Sample Clock timebase.DAQmx_Val_SameAsMasterTimebase10282Use the same source as

### DAQmx_AIConv_Timebase_Src

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AIConv_Timebase_Src

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the terminal of the signal to use as the AI Convert Clock Timebase. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_SameAsSampTimebase | 10284 | Use the same source as Sample Clock timebase. |
| DAQmx_Val_SameAsMasterTimebase | 10282 | Use the same source as the Master Timebase. |
| DAQmx_Val_100MHzTimebase | 15857 | Use the onboard 100 MHz timebase. |
| DAQmx_Val_80MHzTimebase | 14636 | Use the onboard 80 MHz timebase. |
| DAQmx_Val_20MHzTimebase | 12537 | Use the onboard 20 MHz timebase. |
| DAQmx_Val_8MHzTimebase | 16023 | Use the onboard 8 MHz timebase. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAIConvTimebaseSrc](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga4993dfbb8f7fb04d0ecfb78fa81404b2.html)
- [DAQmxSetAIConvTimebaseSrc](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga2c758b1ab257ee3ea0b40cdcaa024656.html)
- [DAQmxResetAIConvTimebaseSrc](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga4613a8a765ae01b1ada2b0ba225f20f9.html)
- [DAQmxGetAIConvTimebaseSrcEx](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga06414145c9ed0ed9449b791ef435f84f.html)
- [DAQmxSetAIConvTimebaseSrcEx](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga07a90a71fd35969d564229f824a46120.html)
- [DAQmxResetAIConvTimebaseSrcEx](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga4d5f0cc0115b9fecbee6c9b74962cdab.html)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_SyncClk_IntervalRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsuInt32Specifies the interval, in Sample Clock periods, between each internal Synchronization Clock pulse. NI-DAQmx uses this pulse for synchronization of triggers between multiple devices at different rates. Refer to device documenta

### DAQmx_SyncClk_Interval

#### Syntax

DAQmx_SyncClk_Interval

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| uInt32 | Specifies the interval, in Sample Clock periods, between each internal Synchronization Clock pulse. NI-DAQmx uses this pulse for synchronization of triggers between multiple devices at different rates. Refer to device documentation for information about how to calculate this value. |  |

In either case, the sample clock does not stop.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_HaltOutputAndError14615Stop generating samples and return an error.D

### DAQmx_SampClk_UnderflowBehavior

#### Syntax

DAQmx_SampClk_UnderflowBehavior

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the action to take when the onboard memory of the device becomes empty. In either case, the sample clock does not stop. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_HaltOutputAndError | 14615 | Stop generating samples and return an error. |
| DAQmx_Val_PauseUntilDataAvailable | 14616 | Pause the task until samples are available in the FIFO. |

- [DAQmxGetSampClkUnderflowBehavior](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gae3a693f013bdc1373b7a01c0d37d6c58.html)

| float64 | Specifies the sampling rate in samples per channel per second. If you use an external source for the Sample Clock, set this input to the maximum expected rate of that clock. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetSampClkRate](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga10478a824efc933e6f62600d5fc127bb.html)

## TOPIC 02296: DAQmx_Trigger_SyncType

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__advanced_1ga61ae0d81667a9bdf3eedaf6e8dc38453.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__advanced_1ga61ae0d81667a9bdf3eedaf6e8dc38453.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_Trigger_SyncTypeRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the role of the device in a synchronized system. Setting this value to DAQmx_Val_Master or DAQmx_Val_Slave enables trigger skew correction. If you enable trigger skew correction, set this property to DAQmx_Val_Master o

### DAQmx_Trigger_SyncType

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Trigger_SyncType

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the role of the device in a synchronized system. Setting this value to DAQmx_Val_Master or DAQmx_Val_Slave enables trigger skew correction. If you enable trigger skew correction, set this property to DAQmx_Val_Master on only one device, and set this property to DAQmx_Val_Slave on the other devices. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_None | 10230 | Disables trigger skew correction. |
| DAQmx_Val_Master | 15888 | Device is the source for shared clocks and triggers. |
| DAQmx_Val_Slave | 15889 | Device uses clocks and triggers from the master device. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetTriggerSyncType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga8e25ed7b0020006e33c6c6e2b5da34bf.html)
- [DAQmxSetTriggerSyncType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gae775bc73948c8df73cbbe6decad58e2c.html)
- [DAQmxResetTriggerSyncType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga39daba7b4fe8d0a283a0ca4b5eb9facf.html)

Parent topic:

Advanced

## TOPIC 02323: DAQmx_PauseTrig_Type

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__more__pause_1gacea47fdf6280fa65e131f514f5e94644.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__more__pause_1gacea47fdf6280fa65e131f514f5e94644.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_PauseTrig_TypeRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the type of trigger to use to pause a task.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_AnlgLvl10101Pause the measurement or generation while an analog signal is above or below a level.DAQmx_Val_AnlgWin10103Pause the measurement or generation

### DAQmx_PauseTrig_Type

#### Syntax

DAQmx_PauseTrig_Type

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the type of trigger to use to pause a task. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_AnlgLvl | 10101 | Pause the measurement or generation while an analog signal is above or below a level. |
| DAQmx_Val_AnlgWin | 10103 | Pause the measurement or generation while an analog signal is either inside or outside of a range of values. |
| DAQmx_Val_DigLvl | 10152 | Pause the measurement or generation while a digital signal is at either a high or low state. |
| DAQmx_Val_DigPattern | 10398 | Pause the measurement or generation while digital physical channels either match or do not match a digital pattern. |
| DAQmx_Val_None | 10230 | Do not pause the measurement or generation. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetPauseTrigType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga3e4edf9a2264599c4d33d7335f0daaf2.html)
- [DAQmxSetPauseTrigType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gafe93835420db8d74cabdf8b6a51e379b.html)
- [DAQmxResetPauseTrigType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga67a396bc76102e154866751a8bde2428.html)

Parent topic:

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__more__pause__analog__level_1gab6d1bee6a8ff0b7510b294d98d18d52e.html`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AnlgLvl_PauseTrig_HystRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies a hysteresis level in the units of the measurement or generation. If Pause When is DAQmx_Val_AboveLvl, the trigger does not deassert until the source signal passes below Level minus the hysteresis. If Pause Whe

### DAQmx_AnlgLvl_PauseTrig_Hyst

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AnlgLvl_PauseTrig_Hyst

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies a hysteresis level in the units of the measurement or generation. If Pause When is DAQmx_Val_AboveLvl, the trigger does not deassert until the source signal passes below Level minus the hysteresis. If Pause When is DAQmx_Val_BelowLvl, the trigger does not deassert until the source signal passes above Level plus the hysteresis. Hysteresis is always enabled. Set this property to a non-zero value to use hysteresis. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAnlgLvlPauseTrigHyst](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga33b22742a17086b652b6d00b7e7d232e.html)
- [DAQmxSetAnlgLvlPauseTrigHyst](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga7c6ff4d6be1a03770daeb2195b76fec4.html)
- [DAQmxResetAnlgLvlPauseTrigHyst](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gaedc7ebd06a101cd300778bb90e30edb6.html)

### DAQmx_AnlgWin_PauseTrig_When

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AnlgWin_PauseTrig_When

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |

When enabled, the analog signal must stay within the trigger window for the min

### DAQmx_AnlgWin_PauseTrig_DigFltr_Enable

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AnlgWin_PauseTrig_DigFltr_Enable

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies whether to apply a digital filter to the digital output of the analog triggering circuitry (the Analog Comparison Event). When enabled, the analog signal must stay within the trigger window for the minimum pulse width before being recognized. Use filtering for noisy trigger signals that transition in and out of the window rapidly. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAnlgWinPauseTrigDigFltrEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga633ae5dcb2f9c65b3e260586ee721b75.html)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_DigPattern_PauseTrig_WhenRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies if the Pause Trigger occurs when the physical channels specified with Source match or differ from the digital pattern specified with Pattern.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_PatternMatches10254Trigger when the physical c

### DAQmx_DigPattern_PauseTrig_When

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DigPattern_PauseTrig_When

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies if the Pause Trigger occurs when the physical channels specified with Source match or differ from the digital pattern specified with Pattern. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_PatternMatches | 10254 | Trigger when the physical channels match the specified pattern. |
| DAQmx_Val_PatternDoesNotMatch | 10253 | Trigger when the physical channels do not match the specified pattern. |

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_RefTrig_TypeRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the type of trigger to use to mark a reference point for the measurement.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_AnlgEdge10099Trigger when an analog signal signal crosses a threshold.DAQmx_Val_AnlgMultiEdge16108Trigger when any of the confi

### DAQmx_RefTrig_Type

#### Syntax

DAQmx_RefTrig_Type

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the type of trigger to use to mark a reference point for the measurement. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_AnlgEdge | 10099 | Trigger when an analog signal signal crosses a threshold. |
| DAQmx_Val_AnlgMultiEdge | 16108 | Trigger when any of the configured analog signals cross their respective thresholds. |
| DAQmx_Val_DigEdge | 10150 | Trigger on the rising or falling edge of a digital signal. |
| DAQmx_Val_DigPattern | 10398 | Trigger when digital physical channels match a digital pattern. |
| DAQmx_Val_AnlgWin | 10103 | Trigger when an analog signal enters or leaves a range of values. The range is in the units of the measurement. |
| DAQmx_Val_Time | 15996 | Trigger when a specified time is reached. |
| DAQmx_Val_None | 10230 | Disable triggering for the task. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetRefTrigType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga2d7db178d8d99a6910ae1bb29fcdf5dd.html)
- [DAQmxSetRefTrigType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga42e6f15d89fcd47cc25771ddd4ebaf88.html)
- [DAQmxResetRefTrigType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga112cd651902d9c96f8344d06b130bb89.html)

## TOPIC 02369: DAQmx_AnlgEdge_RefTrig_Hyst

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__reference__analog__edge_1gaf925296e453b1958347ade34ff18dbfd.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__reference__analog__edge_1gaf925296e453b1958347ade34ff18dbfd.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AnlgEdge_RefTrig_HystRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies a hysteresis level in the units of the measurement. If Slope is DAQmx_Val_RisingSlope, the trigger does not deassert until the source signal passes below Level minus the hysteresis. If Slope is DAQmx_Val_Falling

### DAQmx_AnlgEdge_RefTrig_Hyst

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AnlgEdge_RefTrig_Hyst

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies a hysteresis level in the units of the measurement. If Slope is DAQmx_Val_RisingSlope, the trigger does not deassert until the source signal passes below Level minus the hysteresis. If Slope is DAQmx_Val_FallingSlope, the trigger does not deassert until the source signal passes above Level plus the hysteresis. Hysteresis is always enabled. Set this property to a non-zero value to use hysteresis. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAnlgEdgeRefTrigHyst](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga89bcb2ebfa8d79397770cd35c9b5885e.html)
- [DAQmxSetAnlgEdgeRefTrigHyst](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gaf902947e602d6946a92bfb8a8d103d24.html)
- [DAQmxResetAnlgEdgeRefTrigHyst](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga0cb1b6aa8afa910213d8621d59104e50.html)

Parent topic:

Analog Edge

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AnlgEdge_RefTrig_DigFltr_EnableRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies whether to apply a digital filter to the digital output of the analog triggering circuitry (the Analog Comparison Event). When enabled, the analog signal must stay above or below the trigger level for t

### DAQmx_AnlgEdge_RefTrig_DigFltr_Enable

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AnlgEdge_RefTrig_DigFltr_Enable

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies whether to apply a digital filter to the digital output of the analog triggering circuitry (the Analog Comparison Event). When enabled, the analog signal must stay above or below the trigger level for the minimum pulse width before being recognized. Use filtering for noisy trigger signals that transition in and out of the hysteresis window rapidly. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAnlgEdgeRefTrigDigFltrEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gaf1d9df9e507a85893ae22ba992855da6.html)

- [DAQmxResetAnlgEdgeRefTrigDigFltrEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga5d8c5b37229229b739a04e432cd327e6.html)

### DAQmx_DigPattern_RefTrig_When

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DigPattern_RefTrig_When

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies whether the Reference Trigger occurs when the physical channels specified with Source match or differ from the digital pattern specified with Pattern. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_PatternMatches | 10254 | Trigger when the physical channels match the specified pattern. |
| DAQmx_Val_PatternDoesNotMatch | 10253 | Trigger when the physical channels do not match the specified pattern. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

### DAQmx_DigPattern_RefTrig_Src

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DigPattern_RefTrig_Src

#### Remarks

### DAQmx_RefTrig_RetriggerWin

#### Syntax

DAQmx_RefTrig_RetriggerWin

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies the duration in seconds after each trigger during which the device may trigger. Once the window has passed, the device stops detecting triggers, and the task will stop after the device finishes acquiring post-trigger samples that it already started. Specifying a Retrigger Window of -1 causes the window to be infinite. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

## TOPIC 02401: DAQmx_RefTrig_TrigWin

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_RefTrig_TrigWinRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies the duration in seconds after the task starts during which the device may trigger. Once the window has passed, the device stops detecting triggers, and the task will stop after the device finishes acquiring post-trigg

### DAQmx_RefTrig_TrigWin

#### Syntax

DAQmx_RefTrig_TrigWin

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies the duration in seconds after the task starts during which the device may trigger. Once the window has passed, the device stops detecting triggers, and the task will stop after the device finishes acquiring post-trigger samples that it already started. If no triggers are detected during the entire period, then no data will be returned. Specifying a Trigger Window of -1 causes the window to be infinite. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetRefTrigTrigWin](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga19c1a77f677030608780959af55b8be5.html)
- [DAQmxSetRefTrigTrigWin](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga8e11baa7cf4c451773193e2d9a6131cb.html)
- [DAQmxResetRefTrigTrigWin](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga26a117c7847814b96922f3caff61c513.html)

Parent topic:

More

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-c-api-ref path=group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__reference__more_1gaeabe6493ecf6c42b6b2a21622bf50ed1.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 02402: DAQmx_RefTrig_Retriggerable

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__reference__more_1gaeabe6493ecf6c42b6b2a21622bf50ed1.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__reference__more_1gaeabe6493ecf6c42b6b2a21622bf50ed1.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_RefTrig_RetriggerableRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies whether a finite task resets, acquires pretrigger samples, and waits for another Reference Trigger after the task completes. When you set this property to TRUE, the device will acquire post-trigger samples, reset

### DAQmx_RefTrig_Retriggerable

#### Syntax

DAQmx_RefTrig_Retriggerable

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies whether a finite task resets, acquires pretrigger samples, and waits for another Reference Trigger after the task completes. When you set this property to TRUE, the device will acquire post-trigger samples, reset, and acquire pretrigger samples each time the Reference Trigger occurs until the task stops. The device ignores a trigger if it is in the process of acquiring signals. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetRefTrigRetriggerable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga1d8678af2722aa0ec923e570f19de5c0.html)
- [DAQmxSetRefTrigRetriggerable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga45f4fdbd9bdebd40748d1cbef2427339.html)
- [DAQmxResetRefTrigRetriggerable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gaaf77d28c7d1abce84b2bdaaba9c75528.html)

Parent topic:

More

## TOPIC 02410: DAQmx_AnlgEdge_StartTrig_Hyst

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__start__analog__edge_1gab84b395c8cb31f69f5de6d5111c59f40.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__start__analog__edge_1gab84b395c8cb31f69f5de6d5111c59f40.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AnlgEdge_StartTrig_HystRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies a hysteresis level in the units of the measurement or generation. If Slope is DAQmx_Val_RisingSlope, the trigger does not deassert until the source signal passes below Level minus the hysteresis. If Slope is D

### DAQmx_AnlgEdge_StartTrig_Hyst

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AnlgEdge_StartTrig_Hyst

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies a hysteresis level in the units of the measurement or generation. If Slope is DAQmx_Val_RisingSlope, the trigger does not deassert until the source signal passes below Level minus the hysteresis. If Slope is DAQmx_Val_FallingSlope, the trigger does not deassert until the source signal passes above Level plus the hysteresis. Hysteresis is always enabled. Set this property to a non-zero value to use hysteresis. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAnlgEdgeStartTrigHyst](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gadcbf53a63200e94b2977d8ce8c30412f.html)
- [DAQmxSetAnlgEdgeStartTrigHyst](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gacc3a3cba474958f14f6c43c69484b53c.html)
- [DAQmxResetAnlgEdgeStartTrigHyst](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga43b36e13a2e30b0f1150c0fb4b34bb39.html)

Parent topic:

Analog Edge

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_AnlgEdge_StartTrig_DigFltr_EnableRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies whether to apply a digital filter to the digital output of the analog triggering circuitry (the Analog Comparison Event). When enabled, the analog signal must stay above or below the trigger level for

### DAQmx_AnlgEdge_StartTrig_DigFltr_Enable

#### Syntax

DAQmx_AnlgEdge_StartTrig_DigFltr_Enable

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies whether to apply a digital filter to the digital output of the analog triggering circuitry (the Analog Comparison Event). When enabled, the analog signal must stay above or below the trigger level for the minimum pulse width before being recognized. Use filtering for noisy trigger signals that transition in and out of the hysteresis window rapidly. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetAnlgEdgeStartTrigDigFltrEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gafd8297fecbd33d0dbd65fb77a346918b.html)
- [DAQmxSetAnlgEdgeStartTrigDigFltrEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gad44663e2978f4375e7b178acd3b27b20.html)
- [DAQmxResetAnlgEdgeStartTrigDigFltrEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gaf512957f53ddbe9843c73b78b8039473.html)

Parent topic:

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| char* | Specifies the physical channels to use for pattern matching. The order of the physical channels determines the order of the pattern. If a port is included, the order of the physical channels within the port is in ascending order. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

## TOPIC 02427: DAQmx_StartTrig_RetriggerWin

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__start__more_1ga1d79121f44258a47ff43d36415d54020.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__start__more_1ga1d79121f44258a47ff43d36415d54020.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_StartTrig_RetriggerWinRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies the period of time in seconds after each trigger during which the device may trigger. Once the window has expired, the device stops detecting triggers, and the task will finish after the device finishes acquiri

### DAQmx_StartTrig_RetriggerWin

#### Syntax

DAQmx_StartTrig_RetriggerWin

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies the period of time in seconds after each trigger during which the device may trigger. Once the window has expired, the device stops detecting triggers, and the task will finish after the device finishes acquiring post-trigger samples that it already started. Ensure the period of time specified covers the entire time span desired for retrigger detection to avoid missed triggers. Specifying a Retrigger Window of -1 causes the window to be infinite. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetStartTrigRetriggerWin](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gae80a29d89b34e65af73c938fb0e423ee.html)
- [DAQmxSetStartTrigRetriggerWin](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga89d0dde3c6afe898121ed8c831cc4a07.html)
- [DAQmxResetStartTrigRetriggerWin](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga18b83818fd4e1c306faa1c9140ef066a.html)

Parent topic:

More

## TOPIC 02428: DAQmx_StartTrig_MaxNumTrigsToDetect

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__start__more_1ga3537ee28101f15a902b2831b08a9c96a.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__start__more_1ga3537ee28101f15a902b2831b08a9c96a.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_StartTrig_MaxNumTrigsToDetectRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsuInt32Specifies the maximum number of times the task will detect a start trigger during the task. The number of times a trigger is detected and acted upon by the module may be less than the specified amount if the task s

### DAQmx_StartTrig_MaxNumTrigsToDetect

#### Syntax

DAQmx_StartTrig_MaxNumTrigsToDetect

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| uInt32 | Specifies the maximum number of times the task will detect a start trigger during the task. The number of times a trigger is detected and acted upon by the module may be less than the specified amount if the task stops early because of trigger/retrigger window expiration. Specifying the Maximum Number of Triggers to Detect to be 0 causes the driver to automatically set this value to the maximum possible number of triggers detectable by the device and configuration combination. Note: The number of detected triggers may be less than number of trigger events occurring, because the devices were unable to respond to the trigger. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetStartTrigMaxNumTrigsToDetect](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga2ba6052567dadfa703483980d5662bf8.html)
- [DAQmxSetStartTrigMaxNumTrigsToDetect](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga04bc6f7fb61f3d45594e8ccef0e68604.html)
- [DAQmxResetStartTrigMaxNumTrigsToDetect](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga8f6ac2dbc7386df327966947becfba92.html)

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 02430: DAQmx_StartTrig_TrigWin

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__start__more_1ga77d5b28a9f921d58618f1b83ac7d8a3a.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__trigger__start__more_1ga77d5b28a9f921d58618f1b83ac7d8a3a.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_StartTrig_TrigWinRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies the period of time in seconds after the task starts during which the device may trigger. Once the window has expired, the device stops detecting triggers, and the task will finish after the device finishes acquiring

### DAQmx_StartTrig_TrigWin

#### Syntax

DAQmx_StartTrig_TrigWin

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies the period of time in seconds after the task starts during which the device may trigger. Once the window has expired, the device stops detecting triggers, and the task will finish after the device finishes acquiring post-trigger samples for any triggers detected. If no triggers are detected during the entire period, then no data will be returned. Ensure the period of time specified covers the entire time span desired for trigger detection to avoid missed triggers. Specifying a Trigger Window of -1 causes the window to be infinite. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetStartTrigTrigWin](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gafb5489c259cb7b36fddf47324b6f7b23.html)
- [DAQmxSetStartTrigTrigWin](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga9624b0863b0d0718924daa8318b2b410.html)
- [DAQmxResetStartTrigTrigWin](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga7659450bb816a6e63cbd7fd40897c54d.html)

Parent topic:

More

## TOPIC 02432: DAQmx_StartTrig_Retriggerable

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_StartTrig_RetriggerableRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies whether a finite task resets and waits for another Start Trigger after the task completes. When you set this property to TRUE, the device performs a finite acquisition or generation each time the Start Trigger

### DAQmx_StartTrig_Retriggerable

#### Syntax

DAQmx_StartTrig_Retriggerable

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies whether a finite task resets and waits for another Start Trigger after the task completes. When you set this property to TRUE, the device performs a finite acquisition or generation each time the Start Trigger occurs until the task stops. The device ignores a trigger if it is in the process of acquiring or generating signals. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetStartTrigRetriggerable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga0bbb7a90c7ef6ccce6fabaecc97bb816.html)
- [DAQmxSetStartTrigRetriggerable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga64ea2e9235e1e627b457619ca6107886.html)
- [DAQmxResetStartTrigRetriggerable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga1d33bed766866504d829f0abc66994c5.html)

Parent topic:

More

### DAQmx_Watchdog_DO_ExpirState

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Watchdog_DO_ExpirState

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the state to which to set the digital physical channels when the watchdog task expires. You cannot modify the expiration state of dedicated digital input physical channels. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_High | 10192 | Logic high. |
| DAQmx_Val_Low | 10214 | Logic low. |
| DAQmx_Val_Tristate | 10310 | High-impedance state. You can select this state only on devices with bidirectional lines. You cannot select this state for dedicated digital output lines. On some devices, you can select this value only for entire ports. |
| DAQmx_Val_NoChange | 10160 | Do not change the state of the lines. On some devices, you can select this value only for entire ports. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetWatchdogDOExpirState](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gae35afeedd42e4dd2b34287ad8e7c10bc.html)

When you choose this value, the write ma

### DAQmx_Write_RegenMode

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Write_RegenMode

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies whether to allow NI-DAQmx to generate the same data multiple times. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_AllowRegen | 10097 | Allow NI-DAQmx to regenerate samples that the device previously generated. When you choose this value, the write marker returns to the beginning of the buffer after the device generates all samples currently in the buffer. |
| DAQmx_Val_DoNotAllowRegen | 10158 | Do not allow NI-DAQmx to regenerate samples the device previously generated. When you choose this value, NI-DAQmx waits for you to write more samples to the buffer or until the timeout expires. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetWriteRegenMode](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga56657901e0b033f107f913d06a806a5c.html)

## TOPIC 02464: DAQmx_Write_WaitMode

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__write__advanced_1ga64d46c1cc7b4b7a818aa0c342bb3c0cf.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__write__advanced_1ga64d46c1cc7b4b7a818aa0c342bb3c0cf.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_Write_WaitModeRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies how an NI-DAQmx Write function waits for space to become available in the buffer.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_Poll12524Repeatedly check for available buffer space as fast as possible. This mode allows for the highest sampling r

### DAQmx_Write_WaitMode

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Write_WaitMode

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies how an NI-DAQmx Write function waits for space to become available in the buffer. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_Poll | 12524 | Repeatedly check for available buffer space as fast as possible. This mode allows for the highest sampling rates at the expense of CPU efficiency. |
| DAQmx_Val_Yield | 12525 | Repeatedly check for available buffer space, but yield control to other threads after each check. This mode offers a balance between sampling rate and CPU efficiency. |
| DAQmx_Val_Sleep | 12547 | Check for available buffer space once per the amount of time specified in Sleep Time. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetWriteWaitMode](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gad424d1f103e96ae783fd04ae14a561ea.html)
- [DAQmxSetWriteWaitMode](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gafb23ac43fab4886183206bcb9b86fbf9.html)
- [DAQmxResetWriteWaitMode](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga357b7d1059f61e9855b9311be1772f05.html)

Parent topic:

Advanced

- [DAQmxGetWriteSleepTime](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gad7e44408ee4938f202351e881c3b06e0.html)
- [DAQmxSetWriteSleepTime](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga18a4f0e8379f9adf02d5a00f3e14daa1.html)
- [DAQmxResetWriteSleepTime](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gaf6c9b30e48c8ce4b80b91eb82746696e.html)

Parent topic:

### DAQmx_Write_DigitalLines_BytesPerChan

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Write_DigitalLines_BytesPerChan

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| uInt32 | Indicates the number of Boolean values expected per channel in a sample for line-based writes. This property is determined by the channel in the task with the most digital lines. If a channel has fewer lines than this number, NI-DAQmx ignores the extra Boolean values. | Not Settable |

### NIDAQmx.h

This help describes the NI-DAQmx Library functions, which you can use with National Instruments data acquisition and switch devices to develop instrumentation, acquisition, and control applications.
